 If looking at the profile of a specialist, you should have experience, qualification and expertise in the most important field specials (eg legal or IT officer)
 privet bank or sarkari bank:iske baad yah tay karen ki aap sarkari bank main naukari karnaa chaahate hai yaa privet bank main
 The process of recruitment in these two sectors is completely different from each other
 agar aap sarkari bank main naukari karnaa chaahate hai to aapako IBPS exam qualifi karnaa hoga
 IBPS exam is necessary for those candidates who want to apply in 20 banks in public sector
 haalanki SBI or IDBI public sector ke do aise bank hai jo IBPS ke jariye recruitment nahin karte hai
 SBI conducts the examination itself for recruitment
 privet bank:agar aap privet bank main naukari karnaa chaahate hai to aapako job portels or akhbaar main chhapane vaale vigyapanon par nazren rakhni hongi
 Private banks periodically advertise for recruitment
 iske alaava aap bank kii website par jaakar bhi aplai kar sakate hai
 ICICI Bank for hiring www
 icicicareers
 a portal named com is also created, where you can also apply online after searching the job according to your qualification
 sabase aasaan tarika ye he ki aap PO program main admician le len, jise privet bank or sikkim manipal milakar chalaate hai
 After the end of the program period, the candidates are selected in different banks
 kooparative bank:bharat main kai kooparative bank likhit pariksha or intervyuu ke jariye pio or clerk kii post ke liye recruitment karte hai
 This exam is less competitive as compared to IBPS and SBI exam
